w:rsidRPr="00151B88"><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="Amiri" w:hAnsi="Amiri" w:cs="Amiri"/></w:rPr><w:t xml:space="preserve">1. The user selects Create Store with AI . 2. The system displays the store creation page with a text field and instructions. 3. The user enters a store description. 4. The system validates the description (not empty and contains enough words). 5. The Create Store button becomes active. 6. The user clicks the button. 7. The system sends the description to the AI service. 8. The AI analyzes the description and generates store information such as: store name, description, product categories, mock products, and a template. 9. The system displays the generated results to the user. 10. The user reviews and may edit the results. 11. The user clicks Confirm &amp; Create Store . 12. The system creates the store and links it to the user account. 13. The system shows a success message and redirects the user to the store dashboard. <w:tc><w:tcPr><w:tcW w:w="1795" w:type="dxa"/></w:tcPr><w:p w14:paraId="11223574" w14:textId="79AA3C44" w:rsidR="00522881" w:rsidRPr="00412682" w:rsidRDefault="00DC71D8" w:rsidP="00DC71D8"><w:pPr><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="Amiri" w:eastAsia="Times New Roman" w:hAnsi="Amiri" w:cs="Amiri"/><w:b/><w:bCs/><w:u w:val="single"/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="00412682"><w:rPr><w:rStyle w:val="Strong"/><w:rFonts w:ascii="Amiri" w:hAnsi="Amiri" w:cs="Amiri"/><w:b w:val="0"/><w:bCs w:val="0"/><w:color w:val="0F1115"/><w:shd w:val="clear" w:color="auto" w:fill="FFFFFF"/></w:rPr><w:t>Alternative Flows <w:tcPr><w:tcW w:w="7025" w:type="dxa"/></w:tcPr><w:p w14:paraId="60B02D70" w14:textId="3239528A" w:rsidR="009C3E1F" w:rsidRPr="009C3E1F" w:rsidRDefault="00151B88" w:rsidP="00C16247"><w:pPr><w:rPr><w:rFonts w:ascii="Amiri" w:hAnsi="Amiri" w:cs="Amiri"/><w:u w:val="single"/><w:rtl/></w:rPr></w:pPr><w:r w:rsidRPr="009C3E1F"><w:rPr><w:rStyle w:val="Strong"/><w:rFonts w:ascii="Amiri" w:hAnsi="Amiri" w:cs="Amiri"/><w:b w:val="0"/><w:bCs w:val="0"/><w:u w:val="single"/></w:rPr><w:t xml:space="preserve">A1 – Description Too Short (after step 4 of the main flow ): 5. The system detects that the description is too short. 6. The system shows a message asking the user to enter a better description. 7. The user remains on the same page and enters a new description. ; the flow returns to step 5. A2 - Description Insufficient for AI to Extract Settings ( after step 8 of the main flow): 9. The AI detects that the description is not enough to determine all store settings. 10. The AI asks additional multiple-choice questions. 11. The user selects suitable options. 12. The AI completes the analysis and sends the final settings to the system. 13. The flow returns to step 9 of the main flow. E1 – AI Service Connection Failure (after step 7 of the main flow ): 1. The system fails to connect to the AI service. 2. The system shows an error message. 3. The system opens the product management interface and displays the list of products belonging to the user’s store. If the user chooses to add a new product: 3.1. The system opens the Add Product form. 3.2. The user enters the required information such as product name, description, price, and stock quantity. 3.3. The user may upload one or more product images. 3.4. The system validates the required fields. 3.5. The system saves the product and links it to the current Store ID. 3.6. The system displays the updated product list including the new product. If the user chooses to edit an existing product: 4.1. The system opens the product editing interface with the current product information. 4.2. The user modifies the required fields 4.3. The user may add or remove product images. 4.4. The system saves the updated information. 4.5. The system displays the updated product information in the product list. If the user chooses to delete a product: 5.1. The system asks the user to confirm the deletion process . 5.2. The user confirms the deletion. 5.3. The system deletes the product from the store database. 5.4. The system opens the Add Category form . 3.2 . The user enters the category name and optional description . 3.3 . The system validates the required fields. 3.4 . The system displays the updated category list. If the user chooses to delete a category: 5.1 . The system asks the user to confirm the deletion process . 5.2 . The user confirms the deletion. 5.3 .
